I found the key parts:\n\n1. In `CryptoFacade.resolveSessionKey()` (line 193), the method caches session keys for Mail instances. When a Mail is loaded, its session key is cached for related entities like MailBody and MailDetailsDraft (lines 233-241).\n\n2. The cache uses `setSessionKeyCacheWithTuple()` (line 280) which caches the session key using the elementId part of the tuple.\n\n3. The problem is that when related entities (MailDetailsDraft, MailBody, File) are loaded separately, they rely on the cache for the session key. However, if the cache is cleared or if the entities are loaded before the Mail's session key is resolved, the cache won't have the key.\n\n4.
